country_event = {
	id = bormann.0
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.0" }
	title = bormann.0.t
	desc = bormann.0.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_nazi_street

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = bormann.0.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = bormann.0.a_tt
		hidden_effect = { BOR_Influence_Initialize = yes }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = bormann_kartenhaus.0
	# immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann_kartenhaus.0" }
	title = "Kartenhaus AI Pulse"
	desc = "You shouldn't be seeing this"
	picture = GFX_report_event_nazi_street

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = BOR_Kartenhaus_Active
	}

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		BOR_SIG_AI_BiweeklyCheck = yes
		country_event = { id = bormann_kartenhaus.0 days = 14 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ":)"
	}
}

country_event = { #anti heydrich pact from speer
	id = bormann.8
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.8"}
    title = bormann.8.t
    desc = bormann.8.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_german_army

	trigger = {
		country_exists = HGR
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = bormann.8.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_country_flag = anti_heydrich_pact
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = GGR }
			GGR = { country_event = goering.8 } #continue
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				anti_heydrich_pact_script = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = bormann.8.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = GGR }
			GGR = { country_event = goering.8 } #continue
			SGR = { country_event = speer.19 } #rejected by bormann
		}
		else = {
			SGR = { country_event = speer.17 } #dead in water
		}
	}
}

#The Question of Slavery
country_event = {
	id = bormann.26
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.26" }
	title = bormann.26.t
	desc = bormann.26.desc
	picture = GFX_report_generic_prisoners2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Build ghettos in the cities
		name = bormann.26.a
		BOR_SIG_SP_10_2 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SL_10_2_2 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AP_2_2 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_2_2_1 = yes
		TNO_worsen_slavery_policy_effectiveness_med = yes
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = { is_urban_state = yes }
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			add_manpower = 1000
			set_temp_variable = { state_value_multiplier_temp = 1.05 }
			econ_state_value_change_multiply = yes
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = { is_urban_state = yes }
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			add_manpower = 1000
			set_temp_variable = { state_value_multiplier_temp = 1.05 }
			econ_state_value_change_multiply = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # Restore the slave camps
		name = bormann.26.b
		BOR_SIG_AP_10_2 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_10_2_1 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SP_2_2 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SL_2_2_0 = yes
		TNO_improve_slavery_policy_effectiveness_monthly_low = yes
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = { is_rural_state = yes }
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_manpower = 10000
			add_building_construction = {
				type = prisons
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = { is_rural_state = yes }
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_manpower = 10000
			add_building_construction = {
				type = prisons
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# A Meeting with the Wehrmacht's Leaders
country_event = {
	id = bormann.28
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.28" }
	title = bormann.28.t
	desc = bormann.28.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bormann_wins

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Let's hear them out
		name = bormann.28.a
		country_event = {
			id = bormann.29
			days = 1
		}
		set_variable = { bormann_speidel_point = 0 }
		set_variable = { bormann_schorner_point = 0 }
	}
}

# Speidel VS. Schörner, ROUND 1: FIGHT! - The Future Direction
country_event = {
	id = bormann.29
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.29" }
	title = bormann.29.t
	desc = bormann.29.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bormann_wins

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # We must adapt our strategies to this new age of warfare.
		name = bormann.29.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 
		    modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GER_BOR_ROOT option =  GER_BOR_ROOT_CONSERVATOR }	
			}
		}	
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_BOR_favour_speidel
		country_event = {
			id = bormann.30
			days = 1
		}
		add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
		    name = land_doc_bonus
		    cost_reduction = 0.5
		    uses = 1
		    category = land_doctrine
		}
		add_to_variable = { bormann_speidel_point = 1 }
	}
	option = { # Our strategies won us the war, there's no need to change them.
		name = bormann.29.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 
		    modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GER_BOR_ROOT option =  GER_BOR_ROOT_REFORMIST }	
			}
		}	
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_BOR_favour_schorner
		country_event = {
			id = bormann.30
			days = 1
		}
		add_war_support = 0.075
		add_to_variable = { bormann_schorner_point = 1 }
	}
}

# Speidel VS. Schörner, ROUND 2: FIGHT! - Conscription

		}

			id = bormann.31
			days = 1
		}
		TNO_improve_training_policy_effectiveness_monthly_med = yes
		TNO_worsen_conscription_policy_effectiveness_monthly_med = yes
		add_to_variable = { bormann_speidel_point = 1 }
	}
	option = { # All brave sons of Germany must fight.
		name = bormann.30.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 
		    modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GER_BOR_ROOT option =  GER_BOR_ROOT_REFORMIST }	
			}
		}	
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_BOR_favour_schorner
		country_event = {
			id = bormann.31
			days = 1
		}
		TNO_improve_conscription_policy_effectiveness_monthly_med = yes
		TNO_worsen_training_policy_effectiveness_monthly_med = yes
		add_to_variable = { bormann_schorner_point = 1 }
	}
}

# Speidel VS. Schörner, FINAL ROUND: FIGHT! - The Role of the Wehrmacht
country_event = {
	id = bormann.31
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.31" }

	desc = bormann.31.desc

		    modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GER_BOR_ROOT option =  GER_BOR_ROOT_CONSERVATOR }	
			}
		}		
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_BOR_favour_speidel
		country_event = {
			id = bormann.32
			days = 1
		}
		TNO_improve_training_policy_effectiveness_monthly_low = yes
		add_to_variable = { bormann_speidel_point = 1 }
	}
	option = { # The Wehrmacht should have a political role.
		name = bormann.31.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 
		    modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GER_BOR_ROOT option =  GER_BOR_ROOT_REFORMIST }	
			}
		}	
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_BOR_favour_schorner
		country_event = {
			id = bormann.32
			days = 1
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		TNO_improve_political_parties_policy_effectiveness_monthly_low = yes
		add_to_variable = { bormann_schorner_point = 1 }
	}
}

# The Result
country_event = {
	id = bormann.32
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.32" }
	title = bormann.32.t
	desc = { text = bormann.32.desc_speidel_victory trigger = { check_variable = { bormann_speidel_point > bormann_schorner_point } } }
	desc = { text = bormann.32.desc_schorner_victory trigger = { check_variable = { bormann_schorner_point > bormann_speidel_point } } }
	picture = GFX_report_event_bormann_wins

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Speidel wins
		name = bormann.32.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { bormann_speidel_point > bormann_schorner_point } }
		BOR_SIG_AS_0_15 = yes
		add_ideas = { 
			GER_BOR_speidels_okw
			GER_Hans_Speidel_high_command
		}
		set_country_flag = BOR_speidel_okw
		clear_variable = bormann_speidel_point
		clear_variable = bormann_schorner_point
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = BOR_Dismantlement_I.100 days = 30 } }
	}
	option = { # Schörner wins oh god oh fuck
		name = bormann.32.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { bormann_schorner_point > bormann_speidel_point } }
		BOR_SIG_AS_2_15 = yes
		add_ideas = {
			GER_BOR_schorners_okw
			GER_Ferdinand_Schorner_high_command
		}
		set_country_flag = BOR_schorner_okw
		clear_variable = bormann_speidel_point
		clear_variable = bormann_schorner_point
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = BOR_Dismantlement_I.1 days = 30 } }
	}
}

# Bormann breaks down deals with his allies
country_event = {
	id = bormann.34
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.34" }
	title = bormann.34.t
	desc = bormann.34.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bormann_wins

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # 
		name = bormann.34.a
		BOR_SIG_AP_0_5 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = BOR_militarists_dismantled }
			BOR_SIG_SS_0_10 = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = BOR_reformists_dismantled }
			BOR_SIG_SS_2_10 = yes
		}
		BOR_Influence_Update = yes
	}
}

#Chaos on the Weichsel
country_event = {
	id = bormann.1500
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: bormann.1500" }
	title = bormann.1500.t
	desc = bormann.1500.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_anarchy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	#Pragmatic solution
	option = {
		name = bormann.1500.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 80 
		    modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GER_BOR_POL_NEGOTIATION option =  GER_BOR_POL_NEGOTIATION_WAR }
			}
		}	
		
		BOR_SIG_AL_7_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_8_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_9_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_3_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_2_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SL_4_2_2 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SL_10_2_2 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SL_6_2_2 = yes
		
		add_stability = 0.05

		
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = { id = bormann.1501 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	#Hardline solution
	option = {
		name = bormann.1500.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 
		    modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GER_BOR_POL_NEGOTIATION option =  GER_BOR_POL_NEGOTIATION_RP }
			}
		}	
		
		BOR_SIG_SL_7_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SL_8_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SL_9_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SL_3_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SL_2_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_4_2_2 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_10_2_2 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_6_2_2 = yes
		
		add_war_support = 0.1
		
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = { id = bormann.1511 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.150" }
	title = bormann.1505.t
	desc = bormann.1505.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_agreement
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	#Offer RP Polen
	option = {
		name = bormann.1505.a
		
		BOR_SIG_AL_7_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_8_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_9_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_3_5_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AP_3_5 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SL_4_3_2 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SL_10_3_2 = yes
		
		trigger = { check_variable = { pol_agree = 3 } }
		
		hidden_effect = {
			POL = { country_event = { id = bormann.153 days = 1 } }
			set_country_flag = POL_accepted_protection
		}
		
	}
	
	#Offer GGR 2.0
	option = {
		name = bormann.1505.b
		
		BOR_SIG_SL_7_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SL_8_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SL_9_3_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_SL_3_5_0 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_4_3_2 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AP_4_3 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_10_3_2 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AP_10_3 = yes
		
		trigger = { check_variable = { pol_agree < 3 }  }
		hidden_effect = {
			POL = { country_event = { id = bormann.152 days = 1 } }
			set_country_flag = POL_denied_submission
		}
	}
	
	#Catch cheater!
	option = {
		name = bormann.1505.c
		trigger = { check_variable = { pol_agree > 3 }  }
		add_political_power = -1000
	}
}

#The Polish response arrives in Germania, Warschau Telegram
country_event = {
    id = bormann.154
    immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.154" }
	title = bormann.154.t
    #Polish say yes
    desc = { text = bormann.154.desc_agreed trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_accepted_protection } }
    #Polish say no
    desc = { text = bormann.154.desc_declined trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_denied_submission } }
    picture = GFX_report_event_german_agreement
    fire_only_once = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    #Reichsprotektorat accepted
    option = {
        trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_accepted_protection }
		name = bormann.154.a_accepted
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = { news_event = bormann.155 }
			GGN = { annex_country = { target = POL transfer_troops = no } }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = GGN
				autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_reichskommissariat
			}
			GGN = {
				set_popularities = {
					national_socialism = 80
					fascism = 20
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = RPO_protectorate
				promote_character = GGN_albert_forster
			}
		}
    }

    #Polish say no
    option = {
        trigger = { has_country_flag = POL_denied_submission }
		name = bormann.154.a_declined
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			#modifier = { #This option of GER_BOR_POL_NEG doesn't exist, so comment outed.
			#	factor = 0
			#	has_game_rule = { rule = GER_BOR_POL_NEGOTIATION option =  GER_BOR_POL_NEGOTIATION_GG }
			#}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GER_BOR_POL_NEGOTIATION option =  GER_BOR_POL_NEGOTIATION_RP }
			}
		}		
		BOR_SIG_SP_0_10 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = { news_event = bormann.155 }
			add_timed_idea = { idea = GER_bormann_polish_humiliation  days = 180 }
			country_event = { id = bormann.157 days = 7 } 
		}
    }
}

		}

    }
    option = {
        trigger = {
			GER = { has_country_flag = POL_denied_submission }
			NOT = {
				tag = POL
				tag = GER
				tag = NPL
			}
		}
        name = bormann.155.d_ggn

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.1552"}
    title = bormann.1552.t
    desc = bormann.1552.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = bormann.1552.a
		give_guarantee = SWE
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = SWE
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = BOR_SWE_negotiations
		add_political_power = 200
		SWE = { add_ideas = Pakt_Observer }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = bormann.1647 days = 1} }
		add_stability = 0.1
	}
}

#Look to the North
country_event = {
	id = bormann.1600
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.1600"}
    title = bormann.1600.t
    desc = bormann.1600.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_generic_mountain
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = bormann.1600.a
		
		if = {
			limit = { FIN = { has_government = communist } }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = bormann.1622 days = 3 } }
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = bormann.1601 days = 3 } }
		}
	}
}

#Rearmament
country_event = {
	id = bormann.1602
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.1602"}
    title = bormann.1602.t
    desc = bormann.1602.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_german_arms
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	#Demand full rearmament to Pakt standarts
	option = {
		name = bormann.1602.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = FIN_GER_NEGOTIATION option =  FIN_GER_NEGOTIATION_FAILURE }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_GDP_boost_flat = 2.5 }
		econ_GDP_boost_once_flat = yes
		add_to_variable = { fin_agree = 5 }
		send_equipment = {
			equipment = infantry_equipment
			amount = 5000
			target = FIN
		}

		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = bormann.1603 days = 3 } }
	}
	
	#Just give a discount for finns
	option = {
		name = bormann.1602.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = FIN_GER_NEGOTIATION option =  FIN_GER_NEGOTIATION_SUCCESS }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_GDP_boost_flat = 1 }
		econ_GDP_boost_once_flat = yes
		add_to_variable = { fin_agree = 2 }
		
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = bormann.1605 days = 3 } }
	}
}

				has_game_rule = { rule = FIN_GER_NEGOTIATION option =  FIN_GER_NEGOTIATION_SUCCESS }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { fin_agree = -2 }

		if = {
			limit = {has_country_flag = BOR_scandic_defence_initiative}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = bormann.1617 days = 3 } }
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = bormann.1618 days = 3 } }
		}
	}
	
	#No
	option = {
		name = bormann.1616.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = FIN_GER_NEGOTIATION option =  FIN_GER_NEGOTIATION_FAILURE }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { fin_agree = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {has_country_flag = BOR_scandic_defence_initiative}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = bormann.1617 days = 3 } }
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = bormann.1618 days = 3 } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = bormann.101
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.101"}
    title = bormann.101.t
    desc = bormann.101.d
    picture = GFX_report_event_german_army
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Yea
		name = bormann.101.a
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = has_bormann }
		log = "[This.GetName] accepted Bormann"
		#Effects for country here
	}
	option = { #Nah
		name = bormann.101.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = rejected_bormann
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = CZE
						original_tag = DEN
						original_tag = HOL
						original_tag = MCW
						original_tag = SLO
						original_tag = CZE
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = rejected_bormann }
				}
				country_event = { id = bormann.101 days = 3 random = 24 }
				ROOT = { set_temp_variable = { bormann_option = 1 } }
			}
			#Speer is dead if there's nobody else to flee to
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { bormann_option = 1 } } }
				set_global_flag = bormann_dead
				every_country = {
					news_event = { id = bormann.102 days = 3 random = 24 }
				}
				log = "[This.GetName] rejected Bormann, Bormann dead"
			}
		}
		log = "[This.GetName] rejected Bormann"
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = bormann.652.a
		BOR_SIG_AP_0_3 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AP_6_3 = yes
		HOL = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HOL_SS_in_power }
				add_popularity = { ideology = esoteric_nazism popularity = -0.05 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = ultranationalism 	popularity = -0.05 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = HOL_fascist_independence
						has_country_flag = HOL_musserist_rk
					}
				}
				add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HOL_biesheuvel_government }
				add_popularity = { ideology = despotism popularity = -0.1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HOL_towards_democracy }
				add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democracy 	popularity = -0.02 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = conservative_democracy	popularity = -0.02 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = liberal_democracy 		popularity = -0.02 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = social_democracy 			popularity = -0.02 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = socialist 				popularity = -0.02 }
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = national_socialism popularity = 0.1 }
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_manpower = -2000
		}
		if = {
			limit = { HOL = { has_country_flag = HOL_SS_in_power } }
			country_event = { id = bormann.682 days = 3 }
		}
		else = { country_event = { id = bormann.653 days = 12 } }
	}
}

country_event = { #Bormann slams his fist on the table and reminds Drechsler his place, mentioning how if he doesnt want his whole work to be destroyed he should fall in line. Can either succeed or fail.
	id = bormann.50021
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.50021"}
	title = bormann.50021.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_iberia_meeting_table
	desc = bormann.50021.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = bormann.50021.a
		set_variable = { BOR_drechsler_negotiation_chance = random }
		if = {
		    limit = {
		        has_game_rule = {
			        rule = OST_BOR_NEGOTIATION_ROOT
			        option = OST_BOR_NEGOTIATION_ROOT_PEACE
				  
				}  
			}   
		    set_variable = { BOR_drechsler_negotiation_chance = 100 }
		} 
		if = {
		    limit = {
		        has_game_rule = {
			        rule = OST_BOR_NEGOTIATION_ROOT
			        option = OST_BOR_NEGOTIATION_ROOT_WAR
				  
				}  
			}   
		    set_variable = { BOR_drechsler_negotiation_chance = 0 }
		}  
		IF = {
			limit = { 
				check_variable = {
					var = BOR_drechsler_negotiation_chance
					value = 0.85
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = bormann.50022 }
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = bormann.50023 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Bormann reconsiders the German policy of enforced agrarianism on Norway
	id = bormann.1050

	option = { #They are loyal enough, let them industrialize
		name = bormann.1050.a
		add_political_power = -30
		BOR_SIG_SL_10_3_1 = yes
		BOR_SIG_AL_2_3_0 = yes
		NOR = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NOR_argricultural_devolution
				add_idea = NOR_initial_recovery
			}
			add_resource = {
				type = aluminium
				amount = 2
				state = 110
			}
			set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 1 }
			econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
			TNO_improve_industrial_equipment_low = yes
			TNO_improve_industrial_expertise_low = yes
			TNO_improve_poverty_med = yes
		}
		# ai_chance = { factor = 60 }
	}
	# option = {#Nah
	# 	name = bormann.1050.b
	# 	add_political_power = 60
	# 	BOR_SIG_AP_10_10 = yes

country_event = { #The Coup
	id = bormann.1053

	title = bormann.1053.t
	desc = bormann.1053.desc

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Coup succeeds
		name = bormann.1053.a
		clr_country_flag = NORCoup_successful
		clr_country_flag = NORCoup_failure
		set_politics = { ruling_party = national_socialism }
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = 0.1
		add_political_power = 100
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NOR_consolidation_of_power
			days = 200
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = NOR_Henrik_Rogstad
			set_party_name = { 
				ideology = national_socialism
				long_name = NOR_national_socialism_rogstad_party_long
				name = NOR_national_socialism_rogstad_party
			}
			set_party_name = { 
				ideology = fascism
				long_name = NOR_fascism_rogstad_party_long
				name = NOR_fascism_rogstad_party
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_all_ministers = yes
			}
			add_ideas = {
				NOR_Sverre_Riisns_hog
				NOR_Henrik_Rogstad_for
				NOR_Axel_Heiberg_Stang_eco
				NOR_Karl_Marthinsen_sec
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = {
				id = bormann.1055
				days = 1
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = NORCoup_failure
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = NOR_BOR_PATH option = NOR_BOR_PATH_MILORG_NO_COUP_FAIL }
			}
            modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = NOR_BOR_PATH option = NOR_BOR_PATH_MILORG_NO_COUP_OK }
			} 			
		}
	}
	option = { #Coup fails
		name = bormann.1053.b
		clr_country_flag = NORCoup_successful
		clr_country_flag = NORCoup_failure
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NOR_coup_aftermath
			days = 90
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.08
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_socialism
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = bormann.1054
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = NORCoup_successful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = NOR_BOR_PATH option =  NOR_BOR_PATH_MILORG_COUP_SUCCESS }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_game_rule = { rule = NOR_BOR_PATH option = NOR_BOR_PATH_MILORG_NO_COUP_FAIL }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_game_rule = { rule = NOR_BOR_PATH option = NOR_BOR_PATH_MILORG_NO_COUP_OK }
			}
		}
	}

	}

country_event = { # Negotiations succeed
	id = bormann.1067
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.1067"}
	title = bormann.1067.t
	desc = bormann.1067.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_bormann_wins

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #
		name = bormann.1067.a
		trigger = { tag = GER }
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_garrison_rights 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_economic_program 
			}
			NOR = {
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_pakt_membership } }
					give_military_access = GER
				}
				add_ideas = NOR_BOR_conference_1
			} 
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_garrison_rights 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_economic_program 
			}
			NOR = {
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_pakt_membership } }
					give_military_access = GER
				}
				add_ideas = NOR_BOR_conference_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_garrison_rights 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_economic_program 
			}
			NOR = {
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_pakt_membership } }
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = GER
						relation = docking_rights
						active = yes
					}
				}
				add_ideas = NOR_BOR_conference_3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_garrison_rights 
				has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_economic_program 
			}
			NOR = {
				if = {
					limit = { GER = { has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_pakt_membership } }
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = GER
						relation = docking_rights
						active = yes
					}
				}
				add_ideas = NOR_BOR_conference_4
			}
			transfer_state = 94
			add_state_core = 94
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_pakt_membership }
			add_to_faction = NOR
			transfer_state = 94
			add_state_core = 94
			hidden_effect = {
				NOR = {
					remove_faction_status = yes
					add_ideas = Pakt_Bundnispartner
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_pakt_membership }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = NOR
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			give_guarantee = NOR
			hidden_effect = {
				NOR = {
					remove_faction_status = yes
					add_ideas = Pakt_Observer
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_choose_kopenhagen
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_choose_oslo
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_choose_goteborg
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_garrison_rights
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_garrison_rights
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_economic_program
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_economic_program
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_full_pakt_membership
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_partial_pakt_membership
		clr_country_flag = BOR_NOR_preparing_coup

		set_country_flag = BOR_NOR_negotiation_success
	}
	option = { #
		name = bormann.1067.a
		trigger = { tag = NOR }
	}
}

		}

				factor = 0

		}
	}
}

country_event = { # The actual Oil Crisis starter event for Bormann
	id = bormann.1207
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.1207" }
	title = bormann.1207.t
	desc = bormann.1207.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_germany_court

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Ding dong your economy is gone
		name = bormann.1207.a
		# Econ
		set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = -3 }
		econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_GDP_boost_percentage = -0.08 }
		econ_GDP_boost_once_percentage = yes
		set_temp_variable = { inflation_temp = 1 }
		econ_inflation_change = yes

		# Socdev
		TNO_worsen_admin_efficiency_med = yes
		TNO_worsen_industrial_equipment_med = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_poverty_change = 5 }
		TNO_worsen_poverty_rate_direct = yes
		TNO_worsen_poverty_high = yes

		# Policy effectiveness
		TNO_worsen_trade_laws_policy_effectiveness_high = yes
		TNO_worsen_political_parties_policy_effectiveness_high = yes
		TNO_worsen_public_meetings_policy_effectiveness_high = yes
		TNO_worsen_press_rights_policy_effectiveness_high = yes
		TNO_worsen_vote_franchise_policy_effectiveness_high = yes
		TNO_worsen_training_policy_effectiveness_high = yes
		TNO_worsen_penal_system_policy_effectiveness_high = yes

		# Grossraum
		set_temp_variable = { BOR_Ausgrenzung_Progress_Change = -6 }
		BOR_EconMech_Ausgrenzung_Modify_Progress = yes
		set_temp_variable = { BOR_Ausgrenzung_MonthlyProgress_Change = -0.4 }
		BOR_EconMech_Ausgrenzung_Modify_MonthlyProgress = yes
		set_temp_variable = { BOR_Breitspurbahn_MonthlyProgress_Change = -0.6 }
		BOR_EconMech_Breitspurbahn_Modify_MonthlyProgress = yes

		# Entscheidungsnetzwerk
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = BOR_das_entscheidungsnetzwerk }
			country_event = {
				id = bor_econ.112
				days = 3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = BOR_das_entscheidungsnetzwerk
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = BOR_all_lead_to_germania
					has_completed_focus = BOR_the_cogs_turn
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bor_econ.113
				days = 3
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = bor_econ.114
				days = 3
			}
		}

		# Tree reload
		clr_country_flag = BOR_Phase1
		clr_country_flag = BOR_Phase2
		set_country_flag = BOR_Phase3
		reload_GER_bormann_post_cw_tree = yes
		set_country_flag = BOR_EconMech_OilCrisis
	}
}

country_event = { # UAR bounty time
	id = bormann.1213
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event bormann.1213" }
	title = bormann.1213.t
	desc = bormann.1213.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_arab_soldiers1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = { country_exists = UAR }

	option = { # 
		name = bormann.1213.a
		set_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_pp_bonus = BOR_OC_participation }
		set_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_war_support_bonus = BOR_OC_participation }
		multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_pp_bonus = 3 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_war_support_bonus = 0.001 }
		add_political_power = BOR_OC_pp_bonus
		add_war_support = BOR_OC_war_support_bonus
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { BOR_OC_participation > 30 } }
			set_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = BOR_OC_participation }
			set_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = BOR_OC_participation }
			divide_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = 50 }
			divide_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = 100 }

			# Economic bonuses are proportional to the UAR's size
			if = {
				limit = { UAR = { owns_state = 446 } } # Egypt
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = 1.1 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = 1.05 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { UAR = { owns_state = 294 } } # Oman
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = 1.1 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = 1.05 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { UAR = { owns_state = 293 } } # Yemen
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = 1.1 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = 1.05 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { UAR = { owns_state = 291 } } # Iraq
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = 1.1 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = 1.05 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { UAR = { owns_state = 656 } } # The Gulf
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = 1.1 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = 1.05 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { UAR = { owns_state = 1306 } } # The Levant
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus = 1.1 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus = 1.05 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { money_reserves_temp = BOR_OC_liquid_reserves_bonus }
			econ_money_reserves_change_raw_money = yes
			set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = BOR_OC_gdp_growth_bonus }
			econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { BOR_OC_participation > 60 } }
			UAR = { add_ideas = GER_Bormann_OC_UAR_trade }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { BOR_OC_participation > 80 } }
			UAR = { give_resource_rights = { receiver = GER state = 291 } }
		}
		clear_variable = BOR_OC_participation
	}
}

					limit = {
						USA = { is_faction_leader = yes }
						ITA = { is_in_faction_with = USA }
					}
					add_ideas = OFN_Independent_Member
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes }
						ITA = { is_in_faction_with = JAP }
					}
					add_ideas = Sphere_Coequal
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ITA = { is_faction_leader = yes }
					}
					add_ideas = TRI_Member_Client
				}
			}
			every_country = { news_event = { id = WORLD.664 days = 1 } }
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}
	option = { # Italy rejects France (dunno why a player would choose this, but the option is here if they want to)

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}

					}

				}
			}
			every_country = { news_event = { id = WORLD.664 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # 
		name = bormann.1718.a
		trigger = { tag = GER }
		add_political_power = -25
	}
	option = { # 
		name = bormann.1718.b
		trigger = { tag = ITA }
		add_political_power = 25
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = "Ok"

	}
}
